###########################
# Mexico Events
###########################

add_namespace = mexico
add_namespace = mexicodemocratic

country_event = { # Start up Event
	id = mexico.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.1"}
	title = mexico.1.t
	desc = mexico.1.d
	picture = GFX_federalization_or_centralization

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mexico.1.a
		country_event = {
			id = mexico.1200
			days = 1
		}
	}
}
country_event = { # Start up Event
	id = mexico.1200
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.1200"}
	title = mexico.1200.t
	desc = mexico.1200.d
	picture = GFX_federalization_or_centralization

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mexico.1200.a
	}
}
### assassination attempt on Zapata's life ###
country_event = { # assassination attempt
	id = mexico.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.2"}
	title = mexico.2.t
	desc = mexico.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_zapata_horse

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Zapata lives
		name = mexico.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_MILITARY_JUNTA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_MILITARY_DEMOCRACY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_MILITARY_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_NATIONAL_POPULIST_SINARQUISTA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_NATIONAL_POPULIST_GOLDSHIRT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_NATIONAL_POPULIST_INTEGRALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_zapata_is_alvie_flag
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = MEX_asa_rebellion
			add_idea = MEX_emboldened_ASA
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = MEX_dl_opposition
			add_idea = MEX_emboldened_DL
		}
		add_ideas = MEX_post_assasination_chaos
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.306
				days = 60
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_Elections_Can_occur
	}
	option = { # Zapata dies
		name = mexico.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_TOTALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_COMMUNIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_SYNDICALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_RADICAL_SOCIALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_post_assassination
						option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_SOCIAL_DEMOCRAT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_zapata_is_dead_flag
		
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 9372 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		create_country_leader = {# Eufemio Zapata
			name = "Eufemio Zapata"
			desc = "POLITICS_EUFEMIO_ZAPATA_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Eufemio_Zapata.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = agrarian_socialism_subtype
			traits = { dislikes_politics }
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_Villa_Runs
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.277
				days = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # What does Eufemio do?
	id = mexico.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.3"}
	title = mexico.3.t
	desc = mexico.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_eufemio

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Calles seizes power
		name = mexico.3.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = MEX_calles_purged
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_calles_has_power
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { # Pancho Villa
				name = "Pancho Villa"
				desc = "POLITICS_PANCHO_VILLA_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Pancho_Villa.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = agrarian_socialism_subtype
				traits = { dislikes_politics }
			}
			create_country_leader = {# Eufemio Zapata
				name = "Eufemio Zapata"
				desc = "POLITICS_EUFEMIO_ZAPATA_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Eufemio_Zapata.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = maximato_subtype
				traits = {}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.302
				days = 34
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = MEX_Plutarco_Elias_Calles_hog_tot
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Coalition Government saves democracy
		name = mexico.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.300
				days = 20
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:syndicalist }
				add_to_coalition = yes 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = syn_will_join_coalition_tt
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
				add_to_coalition = yes 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = radsoc_will_join_coalition_tt
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = socdem_will_join_coalition_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = worldnews.455
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Villa's Candidacy
	id = mexico.306
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.306"}
	title = mexico.306.t
	desc = mexico.306.d

		}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # tolenado does authoritarianism
	id = mexico.410
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.410" }
	title = mexico.410.t
	desc = mexico.410.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_syndie_party_congress
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.411
				days = 15
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # allow it
		name = mexico.410.a
		add_political_power = 5
		add_to_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth = 1 }
	}
	
	option = { # do nothing
		name = mexico.410.b
		add_political_power = 5
	}
}

country_event = { # tolenado does authoritarianism
	id = mexico.414
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.414" }
	title = mexico.414.t
	desc = mexico.414.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_army
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # allow it
		name = mexico.414.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		add_to_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth > 2 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexico.416
					days = 14
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth < 2 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexico.415
					days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # do nothing
		name = mexico.414.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = MEX_post_assassination
					option = MEX_POST_ASSASSINATION_ELECTION_COMMUNIST
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 5
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth > 2 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexico.416
					days = 14
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { MEX_toledano_auth < 2 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexico.415
					days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		remove_ideas = MEX_Vicente_Lombardo_Toledano_hog_syn
		add_ideas = MEX_Fidel_Velazquez_hog_syn
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # allow it
		name = mexico.416.a
		create_country_leader = {# Vicente Toledano
			name = "Vicente Toledano"
			desc = "POLITICS_VINCENTE_TOLEDANO_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Vincente_Toledano.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = authcom_subtype
			traits = {}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Vicente Toledano" ruling_only = yes }
			}
			set_country_leader_portrait = {
				portrait = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Vincente_Toledano_Authcom.png"
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = { # Rosendo Salazar
			name = "Rosendo Salazar"
			desc = "POLITICS_ROSENDO_SALAZAR_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Rosendo_Salazar.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = liberalized_syndicalism_subtype
			traits = {}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Vicente_Lombardo_Toledano_hog_tot
			MEX_German_List_Arzubide_for_tot
			MEX_Valentin_Campa_Salazar_eco_tot
			MEX_Hernan_Laborde_Rodriguez_sec_tot
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = MEX_communist_totalist_party
			long_name = MEX_communist_totalist_party_long
			ideology = totalist
		}
		add_ideas = MEX_socialist_democratic_resistance_idea3
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = MEX_asa_rebellion
			add_idea = MEX_asa_resistance_idea2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Campesinos War begins
	id = mexico.42
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.42"}
	title = mexico.42.t
	desc = mexico.42.d
	picture = GFX_the_campesino_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mexico.42.a
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = MEX_campesinos_war_idea
			set_variable = {
				MEX_campesinos_power = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.1000
			} 
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					state = 277
				}
			}
			set_demilitarized_zone = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Sinarquista support
	id = mexico.44
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.44"}
	title = mexico.44.t
	desc = mexico.44.d
	picture = GFX_the_campesino_war

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = MEX_junta_goldshirt_alliance
		OR = {
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mexico.44.a
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = MEX_campesinos_power
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_campesinos_subtract_5
	}
}

country_event = { # Campesinos War - factory sabotaged
	id = mexico.48
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.48"}
	title = mexico.48.t
	desc = mexico.48.d
	picture = GFX_the_campesino_war

	trigger = {
		tag = MEX
		has_authoritarian_government = yes
		has_idea = MEX_campesinos_war_idea
		NOT = {
			has_idea = MEX_campesinos_attack
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = MEX
			industrial_complex > 0
			is_controlled_by = MEX
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}
	immediate = {
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MEX
				industrial_complex > 0
				is_controlled_by = MEX
			}
			save_event_target_as = attack_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = mexico.48.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = MEX_campesinos_attack
			days = 90
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		event_target:attack_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1.0
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 0.5
			has_completed_focus = MEX_socialist_education

			has_completed_focus = MEX_state_atheism
		}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = MEX

		}

			days = 90
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		event_target:attack_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 2.0
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MEX_campesinos_subtract_1
	}
	option = { # Cristero Victory

			}
		}

	id = mexico.59
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.59"}
	title = mexico.59.t
	desc = mexico.59.d
	picture = GFX_the_campesino_war
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			NSW = {
				every_army_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_unit_leader_flag = MEX_rev_leader
					}
					set_nationality = MEX
				}
			}
			every_army_leader = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = mex_counter_revolutionary
						has_trait = mex_gold_shirt
						has_trait = mex_junta_general
					}
				}
				set_nationality = NSW
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = MEX
		has_authoritarian_government = yes
		has_idea = MEX_campesinos_war_idea
		check_variable = {
			MEX_campesinos_power > 25
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = { # Become radical socialist
		name = mexico.59.a
		remove_ideas = MEX_campesinos_war_idea
		clear_variable = MEX_campesinos_power
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_stability = 0.1
		army_experience = 25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
}

					has_war_with = MEX
				}
				white_peace = MEX
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					is_in_faction_with = MEX
					has_war_with = YUC
				}
			}
			white_peace = YUC
		}
		YUC = {
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.66
				days = 22
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Yucatan Wins war with Mexico
	id = mexico.700
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.70"}
	title = mexico.700.t
	desc = mexico.700.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_yucatan_map

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = YUC
		controls_state = 277
		has_war_with = MEX
		NOT = {
				 is_supposed_to_fire_for_tag = yes
			}
	}

	option = { #Restore Socialist Mexico
		name = mexico.700.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Salvador Alvarado"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NSW = {
				every_army_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_unit_leader_flag = MEX_rev_leader
					}
					set_nationality = MEX
				}
			}
			every_army_leader = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = mex_counter_revolutionary
						has_trait = mex_gold_shirt
					}
				}
				set_nationality = NSW
			}
			YUC = {
				every_army_leader = {
					set_nationality = MEX
				}
			}
			MEX = {
				change_tag_from = YUC
			}
			MEX = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				create_country_leader = {# Salvador Alvarado
					name = "Salvador Alvarado"
					desc = "POLITICS_ALVORADO_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Salvador_Alvarado.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = agrarian_socialism_subtype
					traits = {}
				}
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = radical_socialist
							last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
							election_frequency = 60
							elections_allowed = yes
						}
					}
					CURRENT_date > "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = yes
						election_frequency = 60
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened
				set_country_flag = MEX_democracy_survives
				set_politics = {
						ruling_party = radical_socialist
						elections_allowed = yes
						election_frequency = 60
					}
					remove_all_ministers = yes
					add_ideas = MEX_Pancho_Villa_hog_rso
			add_ideas = MEX_Francisco_Mendoza_Palma_for_rso
			add_ideas = MEX_Antonio_Diaz_Soto_y_Gama_eco_rso
			add_ideas = MEX_Genovevo_de_la_O_sec_rso
			}	
			MEX = {
				annex_country = {
			target = YUC
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Dissolve the Mexican Government
		name = mexico.700.b
		add_war_support = 0.02
		YUC = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = MEX
				}
				white_peace = MEX
			}
		}

				}
			}
			white_peace = YUC

				days = 5
			}
		}
	}

		tag = MEX

		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened
			has_country_flag = MEX_the_1942_elections_happened
			has_country_flag = MEX_the_1947_elections_happened

country_event = { # republic or monarchy
	id = mexico.108
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.108"}
	title = mexico.108.t
	desc = mexico.108.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_crown

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # maintain the republic
		name = mexico.108.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Salvador Abascal"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Jose Vasconcelos" ruling_only = yes }
			}
			set_country_leader_portrait = {
				portrait = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Jose_Vasconcelos_President.png"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = MEX_organic_cristeros
				}
			}
			complete_national_focus = MEX_ASA_republic_maintained
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MEX_organic_cristeros
			}
			set_country_flag = MEX_IntegroSynarchist_Republic
		}
	}
	
	option = { # restore the monarchy
		name = mexico.108.b
		set_cosmetic_tag = MEX_REGENCY
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = MEX_organic_cristeros
				}
			}
			complete_national_focus = MEX_ASA_monarchy_restored
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MEX_organic_cristeros
			}
			set_country_flag = MEX_Monarchy_Restored
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = MEX_SynarchoIntegralist_Monarchy
				add_ideas = MEX_ASA_an_organic_monarchy
				country_event = {
					id = mexico.360
					days = 12
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				name = "Luis María Martínez"

					days = 20

				name = "Miguel Dario"

		}

			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "José de Jesús"
				desc = "POLITICS_JESUS_ARCHBISHOP_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Jose_de_Jesus.png"

				ideology = authoritarian_democrat

			}

			}

				ideology = market_liberal

			}

				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}

					}

		}

country_event = { # mexicali movement takes power
	id = mexico.184
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico.184"}
	title = mexico.184.t
	desc = mexico.184.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_aztec_icon

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # yay
		name = mexico.184.a
		add_stability = 0.01
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Frida Kahlo"
			desc = "POLITICS_KAHLO_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Frida_Kahlo.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = mexicayotlism_subtype
			traits = {  }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = MEX_kahlo_party
			long_name = MEX_kahlo_party_long
			ideology = radical_socialist
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Pancho_Villa_hog_rso
			MEX_Juana_Belen_Gutierrez_de_Mendoza_for_rso
			MEX_Lazaro_Cardenas_eco_rso
			MEX_Ricardo_Flores_Magon_sec_syn
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_army_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = mex_gold_shirt
			}
			set_nationality = NSW
		}
		NSW = {
			every_army_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_unit_leader_flag = MEX_rev_leader
				}
				set_nationality = MEX
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MEX_AZTEC_EMPIRE #im too lazy to adjust for the other 8 flags
	}
	
	option = { # yay
		name = mexico.184.b
		add_stability = 0.01
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Frida Kahlo"
			desc = "POLITICS_KAHLO_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Frida_Kahlo.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = mexicayotlism_subtype
			traits = {  }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = MEX_kahlo_party
			long_name = MEX_kahlo_party_long
			ideology = radical_socialist
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Pancho_Villa_hog_rso
			MEX_Juana_Belen_Gutierrez_de_Mendoza_for_rso
			MEX_Lazaro_Cardenas_eco_rso
			MEX_Ricardo_Flores_Magon_sec_syn
		}
		every_army_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = mex_gold_shirt
			}
			set_nationality = NSW
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_army_leader = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = mex_gold_shirt
			}
			set_nationality = NSW
		}

		tag = MEX
		has_socialist_government = yes

			has_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened
		}

	immediate = {

			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Frida Kahlo"

				name = "Frida Kahlo"

				picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Frida_Kahlo.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = syn_mexicayotlism_subtype
				traits = {  }
			}

				name = "Frida Kahlo"
				desc = "POLITICS_KAHLO_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MEX/Portrait_Mexico_Frida_Kahlo.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = tot_mexicayotlism_subtype
				traits = {  }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Tot
		name = mexico.197.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened

	option = { # Synd
		name = mexico.197.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened
		}
		set_country_flag = MEX_democracy_survives
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		add_ideas = MEX_Gerardo_Murillo_Cornado_hog_syn
	}
	option = { # Villa
		name = mexico.197.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MEX_the_1937_elections_happened
		}

country_event = {
	id = mexicodemocratic.10
	title = mexicodemocratic.10.title
	desc = mexicodemocratic.10.desc
	picture = GFX_republic_or_monarchy
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.10.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_DEM_presidency
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		set_country_flag = democratic_republic
		set_country_flag = new_constitution
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
						has_country_flag = strong_executive
				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexicodemocratic.122
					days = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = weak_executive

				}
				country_event = {
					id = mexicodemocratic.133
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}	
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.10.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = MEX_DEM_restored_monarchy
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		set_country_flag = mexican_monarchy
		set_country_flag = new_constitution
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = weak_executive
				} 
				country_event = {
					id = mexicodemocratic.155
					days = 2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = strong_executive
				} 
				country_event = {
					id = mexicodemocratic.144
					days = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = mexico.2424
				days = 122
			}	
		}
	}
}

##Event: Constitutional Monarchy
country_event = {
	id = mexicodemocratic.144
	title = mexicodemocratic.14.title
	desc = mexicodemocratic.14.desc
	picture = GFX_constitutional_monarchy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.14.a
		load_focus_tree = mexican_focus
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_create_constitutional_monarchy = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = MEXK
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.14.b
		load_focus_tree = mexican_focus
		MEX_create_constitutional_monarchy = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MEX_cristero_victory_very_cool
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEE_moctemzuma	
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = MEX_cristero_victory_very_cool
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MEE	
		}
	}
}

##Event: Elections 1936
country_event = {
	id = mexicodemocratic.16
	title = mexicodemocratic.16.title
	desc = mexicodemocratic.16.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexico_election
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = MEX_first_election
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "María I"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.16.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_authoritarian_democrats_win = yes
		add_ideas = MEX_Juan_Andreu_Almazan_hog_ade
		add_ideas = MEX_Melchor_Ortega_Camarena_for_ade
		add_ideas = MEX_Victorino_Barcenas_eco_ade
		add_ideas = MEX_Ruben_Salazar_Mallen_sec_ade
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05}
		set_country_flag = MEX_PRUN_term_1
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.16.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_social_conservatives_win = yes
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Manuel_Gomez_Morin_hog_sco
			MEX_Juan_Lascurian_for_sco
			MEX_Luis_Montes_de_Oca_eco_sco
			MEX_Efrain_Gonzalez_Luna_sec_sco
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05}
		set_country_flag = MEX_PAN_term_1
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.16.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_market_liberals_win = yes
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Adolfo_de_la_Huerta_hog_mli
			MEX_Jamie_Bodet_for_mli
			MEX_Antonio_Martinez_Baez_eco_mli
			MEX_Hector_Perez_Martinez_sec_mli
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05}
		set_country_flag = MEX_PLC_term_1
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.16.d
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_social_liberals_win = yes
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			MEX_Manuel_Avila_Camacho_hog_sli
			MEX_Francisco_Castillo_Najera_for_sli
			MEX_Eduardo_Aranzolo_eco_sli
			MEX_Primo_Villa_Michel_sec_sli
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05}
		set_country_flag = MEX_PCP_term_1
	}
	option = {
		name = mexicodemocratic.16.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 1}
		MEX_social_democrats_win = yes
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = MEX_Lazaro_Cardenas_hog_sde
		add_ideas = MEX_Primo_Villa_Michel_for_sde
		add_ideas = MEX_Alberto_J_Pani_eco_sde
		add_ideas = MEX_Jose_Aguilar_y_Maya_sec_sde
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05}
		set_country_flag = MEX_PLM_term_1
	}
}

#########################################################
###### TAKING CALI AND TEXAS BACK FROM THE YANQUIS ######
#########################################################

add_namespace = mexico_req

country_event = {
	id = mexico_req.9
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico_req.9"}
	title = mexico_req.9.t
	desc = mexico_req.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_cession

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { ####Reclaim Territories
		name = mexico_req.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = MEX_reconquista_path
					option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_PEACE
				}
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 375 #Northern Texas
					add_state_claim = 376 #New Mexico
					add_state_claim = 1161 #New Mexico
					add_state_claim = 377 #Arizona
					add_state_claim = 378 #Northern California
					add_state_claim = 379 #Nevada
					add_state_claim = 1165 #reno
					add_state_claim = 797 #San Francisco
					add_state_claim = 798 #Los Angeles
					add_state_claim = 829 #Southern California
					add_state_claim = 833 #Southern Texas
					add_state_claim = 1174 #Tucson
					add_state_claim = 380 #Tucson
					add_state_claim = 1096 #Tucson
					add_state_claim = 1175 #Tucson
					add_state_claim = 1166 #Trans-Pecos
		add_political_power = 40
	}
	option = { ###Let's not claim anything and be nice
		name = mexico_req.9.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_CEDE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_WAR
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_FEDS
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		set_country_flag = MEX_Peace
	}
}

country_event = { ####American Reaction
	id = mexico_req.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico_req.10"}
	title = mexico_req.10.t
	desc = mexico_req.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_cession

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { ### Cede Territories
		name = mexico_req.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND =  {
					NOT = { 
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MEX_reconquista_path
							option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_CEDE
						}
					}
					MEX = { is_ai = yes }
					USA = { is_ai = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_WAR
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_FEDS
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -400
		MEX = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 375 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 375 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 376 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 376 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1161 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1161 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 377 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 377 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 378 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 378 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 379 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 379 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 797 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 797 }
			}	
			if = { 
				limit = { 798 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 798 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 829 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 829 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 833 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 833 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1174 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1174 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 380 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 380 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1096 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1096 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1165 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1165 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1175 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1175 }
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { 1166 = { OR = { is_controlled_by = USA is_controlled_by = WCC } } } 
				MEX = {	transfer_state = 1166 }
			}
		}
		MEX = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1 id = mexico_req.27
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = conq
	}
	option = { ### NEVER!!!!
		name = mexico_req.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_CEDE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_FEDS
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1 id = mexico_req.11
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
	}
	option = { ### agree, for a price
		name = mexico_req.10.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND =  {
					NOT = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MEX_reconquista_path
							option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_FEDS
						}
					}
					MEX = { is_ai = yes }
					USA = { is_ai = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_CEDE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MEX_reconquista_path
						option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_WAR
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1 id = mexico_req.110
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

country_event = { #####American Offer
	id = mexico_req.110
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico_req.110"}
	title = mexico_req.110.t
	desc = mexico_req.110.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_cession

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { ###agree
		name = mexico_req.110.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = TEX
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = CAL
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = WCC
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		give_military_access = WCC
		set_country_flag = MEX_Reconquista
		set_country_flag = MEX_WCC_Alliance
		set_global_flag = MEX_WCC_Alliance
		add_political_power = 100
		
	}
	option = { ###Pussy out
		name = mexico_req.110.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = MEX_reconquista_path
					option = MEX_RECONQUISTA_PATH_FEDS
				}
			}
		}
		MEX = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1 id = mexico_req.11
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #####mexico_req declared war on us omg!
	id = mexico_req.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mexico_req.12"}

	desc = mexico_req.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_mexican_cession

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { ###Lets get some free stuff
		name = mexico_req.12.a
		add_political_power = -40

		if = {
			limit = {
				375 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			load_oob = USA_ANTI_MEX1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				797 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			load_oob = USA_ANTI_MEX2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				377 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			load_oob = USA_ANTI_MEX3
		}

	}
}
